    <h1 class="title-article" id="articleContentId">
     JavaScript 游戏构建指南（二）
    </h1>
   </div>
  </div>
 </div>
 <article class="baidu_pl">

     <path d="M5,0 0,2.5 5,5z" id="raphael-marker-block" stroke-linecap="round" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">
     </path>
    </svg>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      原文：
      <a href="https://zh.book4you.org/book/3426905/60f929" rel="nofollow">
       Building JavaScript games
      </a>
     </p>
     <p>
      协议：
      <a href="http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-nc-sa/4.0/" rel="nofollow">
       CC BY-NC-SA 4.0
      </a>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h2>
     <a id="_6">
     </a>
     七、基本游戏对象
    </h2>
    <p>
     在这一章中，你开始更多地组织画师游戏的源代码。这是必要的，因为一个游戏的源代码包含许多行代码。在前面的例子中，您开始对不同对象上的变量进行分组(例如
     <code>
      Canvas2D
     </code>
     或
     <code>
      cannon
     </code>
     )。在本章中，您将继续通过使用更多的对象和将代码拆分到不同的文件来构建您的代码。
    </p>
    <p>
     使用单独的 JavaScript 文件
    </p>
    <p>
     您可能已经注意到的一件事是，您的 JavaScript 文件变得相当大。拥有一个包含所有代码的大文件并不理想，因为这样很难找到程序的某些部分。将代码拆分到多个源文件中更有意义。一个好的方法是将不同的 JavaScript 对象分割到不同的 JavaScript 文件中，这样每个 JavaScript 文件都包含其中一个对象的代码。Painter3 示例程序包含前面章节中介绍的对象，但是每个对象都在自己的 JavaScript 文件中描述。现在浏览代码和理解程序的结构变得容易多了。您甚至可以将这些文件放在单独的目录中，以指示哪些对象属于同一个目录。例如，您可以将
     <code>
      Keyboard
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      Mouse
     </code>
     JavaScript 文件放在一个名为
     <code>
      input
     </code>
     的目录中。这样，很明显这两个文件都包含与处理输入相关的代码。
    </p>
    <p>
     在浏览器中加载这些独立的 JavaScript 文件有点棘手。在前面的示例中，您已经看到了加载 JavaScript 文件的以下代码行:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"FlyingSpriteWithSound.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您可能希望通过在 HTML 文件中添加更多的这些
     <code>
      script
     </code>
     元素来加载 Painter3 程序中使用的 JavaScript 文件，如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"input/Keyboard.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"input/Mouse.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"Canvas2D.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"system/Keys.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"Painter.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"Cannon.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     不幸的是，如果你试图采用这种添加越来越多
     <code>
      script
     </code>
     元素的方法，你会遇到麻烦。因为 JavaScript 文件是从某个地方的服务器上检索的，所以没有办法确定哪个 JavaScript 文件将首先完成加载。假设浏览器可以加载的第一个文件是
     <code>
      Painter.js
     </code>
     。浏览器无法解释该文件中的代码，因为代码
     <em>
      引用了其他文件
     </em>
     中的代码(如
     <code>
      Canvas2D
     </code>
     对象)。这也适用于其他文件。因此，为了实现这一点，您需要确保文件以某种顺序加载，使得
     <em>
      尊重文件
     </em>
     之间现有的依赖关系。换句话说:如果文件 A 需要文件 B，你需要在文件 A 之前加载文件 B。
    </p>
    <p>
     在 JavaScript 中，可以修改 HTML 页面；因此，理论上，您可以向 HTML 页面添加一个额外的 script 元素，然后开始加载另一个 JavaScript 文件。通过巧妙使用事件处理程序，您可以想象编写 JavaScript 代码，以预定义的顺序加载其他 JavaScript 文件。您也可以使用其他人已经编写的代码，而不是自己编写所有这些代码。这是结构化代码的另一个优点:它使代码对其他应用更有用。
    </p>
    <p>
     对于这本书，我选择使用一个名为
     <em>
      LABjs
     </em>
     (
     <code>
      http://labjs.com/
     </code>
     )的动态脚本加载工具。这是一个非常简单的脚本，可以让您动态地按照预定义的顺序加载其他 JavaScript 文件。下面是使用 LABjs 按照正确的顺序加载所有 JavaScript 文件的代码:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script src<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"../LAB.min.js"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
    $<span class="token constant">LAB</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">script</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'input/Keyboard.js'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">wait</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">script</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'input/Mouse.js'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">wait</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">script</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'Canvas2D.js'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">wait</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">script</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'system/Keys.js'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">wait</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">script</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'Painter.js'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">wait</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">script</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'Cannon.js'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">wait</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">start</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'mycanvas'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>script<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     如您所见，使用 LABjs 非常简单。您只需调用一系列的
     <code>
      script
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      wait
     </code>
     方法。最后一个
     <code>
      wait
     </code>
     方法调用获取一个要执行的函数作为参数。在这个函数中，你开始游戏。通过改变
     <code>
      script
     </code>
     方法调用的顺序，您可以改变脚本加载的顺序。当您开发游戏或其他更大的 JavaScript 应用时，使用这样的脚本非常有用，因为它使得开发和维护代码更加容易。有关显示加载不同 JavaScript 文件的完整示例，请参见 Painter3。这里的另一个改进是我将画布元素的名称作为参数传递给了
     <code>
      start
     </code>
     方法。这样，JavaScript 游戏代码可以使用任何画布名称。
    </p>
    <p>
     你可能不希望游戏的最终(发布)版本使用这样的方法，因为浏览器将不得不加载许多 JavaScript 文件。此时，最好使用另一个程序将所有 JavaScript 文件合并成一个大文件，这样加载速度会更快。此外，通常的做法是对代码结构进行一些优化，使脚本文件尽可能小。这个过程叫做
     <em>
      缩小
     </em>
     。第三十章更详细地讨论了这一点。
    </p>
    <p>
     以错误的方式加载游戏素材
    </p>
    <p>
     之前，我谈到了浏览器以任意顺序加载文件，因为这些文件必须从服务器中检索。同样的规则也适用于加载游戏资源，比如精灵和声音。这是你到目前为止用来加载游戏素材的方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> sprite <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprite<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"someImageFile.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> anotherSprite <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
anotherSprite<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"anotherImageFile.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// and so on</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     看起来很简单。对于每个你想要加载的精灵，你创建一个
     <code>
      Image
     </code>
     对象，并给它的
     <code>
      src
     </code>
     变量赋值。将
     <code>
      src
     </code>
     变量设置为某个值并不意味着图像会立即加载。它只是告诉浏览器开始从服务器检索图像。根据互联网连接的速度，这可能需要一段时间。如果您尝试过早绘制图像，浏览器将会因为访问错误(尝试绘制尚未加载的图像)而停止脚本。为了避免这个问题，在前面的例子中精灵是这样加载的:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> spriteFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_background.jpg"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_barrel <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_barrel<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> spriteFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_barrel.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> spriteFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_red.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> spriteFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_green.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_blue <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_blue<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> spriteFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_blue.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">initialize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
window<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setTimeout</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mainLoop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     注意最后一行代码，粗体。在设置了所有
     <code>
      Image
     </code>
     对象的
     <code>
      src
     </code>
     变量之后，您告诉浏览器在执行主循环之前等待 500 毫秒。这样，浏览器应该有足够的时间来加载精灵。但是网速太慢怎么办？那么 500 毫秒可能不够。或者网速真的很快怎么办？那么你让玩家不必要地等待。为了解决这个问题，您需要程序在执行主循环之前等待所有图像都已加载。您将看到如何使用事件处理函数正确地做到这一点。但在此之前，让我们再多谈一点关于方法和函数的内容。
    </p>
    <p>
     方法和功能
    </p>
    <p>
     您已经看到并使用了相当多不同种类的方法和函数。例如，
     <code>
      Canvas2D.drawImage
     </code>
     方法和
     <code>
      cannon.update
     </code>
     方法之间有一个明显的区别:后者没有任何参数，而前者有(精灵、它的位置、它的旋转和它的原点)。此外，一些函数/方法可以有一个对象的
     <em>
      结果值，该值可以在执行方法调用的指令中使用——例如，通过将结果存储在一个变量中:
     </em>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> n <span class="token operator">=</span> Math<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">random</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     这里，您调用被定义为
     <code>
      Math
     </code>
     对象的一部分的
     <code>
      random
     </code>
     函数，并将它的结果存储在变量
     <code>
      n
     </code>
     中。显然，
     <code>
      random
     </code>
     提供了一个可以存储的结果值。另一方面，
     <code>
      Canvas2D.drawImage
     </code>
     方法不提供可以存储在变量中的结果。当然，这个方法确实有某种效果，因为它在屏幕上绘制了一个精灵，这也可以被认为是方法调用的结果。然而，当我谈论一个方法的
     <em>
      结果
     </em>
     时，我并不是说这个方法对一个对象有某种影响。我的意思是
     <em>
      方法调用
     </em>
     返回一个可以存储在变量中的值。这也称为方法或函数的
     <em>
      返回值
     </em>
     。在数学中，函数有结果是很常见的。数学函数
     <img alt="image" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/0d929a1b8273f3ea4d1e93665b1ca600.jpeg">
      将
      <em>
       x
      </em>
      值作为参数，并返回其平方值作为结果。如果你愿意，你可以用 JavaScript 写这个数学函数:
     </img>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> <span class="token function-variable function">square</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">x</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> x<span class="token operator">*</span>x<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     如果你看看这个方法的头，你会看到它有一个名为
     <code>
      x
     </code>
     的参数。因为函数返回值，所以可以将该值存储在变量中:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> sx <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">square</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     该指令执行后，变量
     <code>
      sx
     </code>
     将包含值 100。在函数体中，您可以使用关键字
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     来指示函数返回的实际值。在
     <code>
      square
     </code>
     的情况下，函数返回表达式
     <code>
      x*x
     </code>
     的结果。注意，执行
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     指令也会终止函数中其余指令的执行。放置在和
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     指令之后的任何指令都不会被执行。例如，考虑以下函数:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> <span class="token function-variable function">someFunction</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token number">12</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">var</span> tmp <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">45</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这个例子中，第二条指令(
     <code>
      var tmp = 45;
     </code>
     )永远不会被执行，因为它之前的指令结束了函数。这是
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     指令的一个非常方便的特性，您可以将它用于您的优势:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> <span class="token function-variable function">squareRoot</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">x</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>x <span class="token operator">&lt;</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token comment">// Calculate the square root, we are now sure that x &gt;=0.</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这个例子中，您使用
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     指令来防止方法用户的错误输入。您不能计算负数的平方根，所以在您进行任何计算或引发任何恼人的、潜在的难以调试的错误之前，您需要处理
     <code>
      x
     </code>
     为负的情况。
    </p>
    <p>
     没有返回值的方法的一个例子是
     <code>
      cannon.handleInput
     </code>
     。因为这个方法没有返回值，所以不需要在方法体中使用
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     关键字，尽管这样做有时还是有用的。例如，假设您只想在鼠标位于屏幕左侧时更改大炮的颜色。您可以通过以下方式实现这一点:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">handleInput</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Keyboard<span class="token punctuation">.</span>keyDown <span class="token operator">===</span> Keys<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token constant">R</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Keyboard<span class="token punctuation">.</span>keyDown <span class="token operator">===</span> Keys<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token constant">G</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token comment">// etc.</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这个方法中，首先检查鼠标的 x 位置是否大于 10。如果是这种情况，就执行
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     指令。此后的任何指令将不再执行。
    </p>
    <p>
     请注意，无论何时调用没有返回值的方法，它都没有可以存储在变量中的结果。例如:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> what <span class="token operator">=</span> cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     因为
     <code>
      cannon.handleInput
     </code>
     没有返回值，所以在这条指令执行后，变量
     <code>
      what
     </code>
     将具有值
     <code>
      undefined
     </code>
     。
    </p>
    <p>
     如果一个方法或函数有一个返回值，这个值不一定要存储在变量中。你也可以直接在
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令中使用它，就像你在
     <code>
      cannon.handleInput
     </code>
     方法中所做的一样:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Math<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">random</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">0.5</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">// do something</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     这里，
     <code>
      Math.random
     </code>
     方法返回一个数字，如果该数字大于 0.5，则执行
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令的主体。有值的东西和没有值的东西之间的区别是你以前见过的:这和你在
     <em>
      指令
     </em>
     (没有值)和
     <em>
      表达式
     </em>
     (有值)之间看到的区别是一样的。所以，这意味着
     <code>
      Math.random()
     </code>
     是一个
     <em>
      表达式
     </em>
     ，而
     <code>
      cannon.handleInput();
     </code>
     是一个
     <em>
      指令
     </em>
     。这两者之间的第二个区别是，表达式从不以分号结尾，而指令总是以分号结尾，除非指令是一个块。
    </p>
    <p>
     声明与参数
    </p>
    <p>
     变量的声明与写在方法头中的参数有很多共同之处。事实上，这些参数也是声明，但是有一些不同:
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      变量在方法体中声明；参数在方法头的括号中声明。
     </li>
     <li>
      变量通过使用赋值指令来获取值；调用方法时，参数会自动获取一个值。
     </li>
     <li>
      变量声明以单词
      <code>
       var
      </code>
      开头；参数声明不会。
     </li>
     <li>
      变量声明以分号结束；参数声明不会。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     以正确的方式加载游戏素材
    </p>
    <p>
     为了让 sprite 加载更容易一点，让我们给
     <code>
      Game
     </code>
     对象添加一个方法
     <code>
      loadSprite
     </code>
     :
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">loadSprite</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">imageName</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">var</span> image <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    image<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> imageName<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> image<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     加载不同精灵的代码现在变得更短了:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> sprFolder <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">"../../assets/Painter/sprites/"</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background <span class="token operator">=</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_background.jpg"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_barrel <span class="token operator">=</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_barrel.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red <span class="token operator">=</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_red.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green <span class="token operator">=</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_green.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_blue <span class="token operator">=</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprFolder <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token string">"spr_cannon_blue.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     然而，处理加载精灵所花费的时间的问题还没有解决。为了解决这个问题，你需要做的第一件事就是记录你加载了多少精灵。这可以通过向
     <code>
      Game
     </code>
     对象添加一个名为
     <code>
      spritesStillLoading
     </code>
     的变量来实现:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> Game <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">spritesStillLoading</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     最初，该变量被设置为值 0。每次加载一个 sprite，变量就增加 1。从逻辑上来说，您可以在
     <code>
      loadSprite
     </code>
     方法中这样做:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">loadSprite</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">imageName</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">var</span> image <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    image<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> imageName<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>spritesStillLoading <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> image<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     所以现在，每次你加载一个精灵，
     <code>
      spritesStillLoading
     </code>
     变量就会增加。接下来，每当一个精灵完成加载时，你想要
     <em>
      减少
     </em>
     这个变量。这可以通过使用事件处理函数来完成。您将这个函数分配给
     <code>
      image
     </code>
     对象中的变量
     <code>
      onload
     </code>
     。在函数体中，变量递减。下面是添加事件处理程序的
     <code>
      loadSprite
     </code>
     方法的版本:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">loadSprite</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">imageName</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">var</span> image <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Image</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    image<span class="token punctuation">.</span>src <span class="token operator">=</span> imageName<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>spritesStillLoading <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    image<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">onload</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>spritesStillLoading <span class="token operator">-=</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> image<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     现在
     <code>
      spritesStillLoading
     </code>
     变量准确地表示了还有多少精灵需要被加载。您可以使用该信息等待主循环的开始，直到该变量包含值 0。为此，您需要创建两个循环方法:一个素材加载循环和一个主游戏循环。在素材加载循环中，您只需检查是否还有必须加载的精灵。如果是这种情况，您再次调用素材加载循环。如果所有的精灵都已经被加载，你调用主循环方法。下面是素材加载循环方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">assetLoadingLoop</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>spritesStillLoading <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        window<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setTimeout</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>assetLoadingLoop<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1000</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">initialize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">mainLoop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您使用
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令来检查仍在加载的精灵数量是否大于 0。如果是这种情况，您在短暂的延迟后再次调用
     <code>
      assetLoadingLoop
     </code>
     方法。一旦所有的精灵都被加载，就会执行
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令的
     <code>
      else
     </code>
     部分。在这一部分中，您调用了
     <code>
      Game
     </code>
     对象中的
     <code>
      initialize
     </code>
     方法，然后调用了
     <code>
      mainLoop
     </code>
     方法。在
     <code>
      initialize
     </code>
     方法中，所有的游戏对象都被初始化(在本例中，只有
     <code>
      cannon
     </code>
     对象)。在加载完所有精灵后进行初始化是很有用的，因为精灵数据在初始化对象时可能会很有用。例如，如果你想计算一个覆盖图的位置，使它画在屏幕的中心，你需要知道精灵的宽度和高度。该信息仅在精灵完成加载时可用。有关完整的概述，请参见 Painter3 示例，该示例阐释了新的 sprite 加载代码。
    </p>
    <p>
     编写一个更有效的游戏循环
    </p>
    <p>
     到目前为止，您已经使用了
     <code>
      window.setTimeout
     </code>
     方法来创建一个运行的游戏循环。虽然这段代码很好，但不幸的是它不是很高效。大多数浏览器提供了一种更有效的方式来实现这一点，这种方式专门针对交互式绘图应用，如游戏。问题是，并不是所有的浏览器和版本都使用相同的方法名。最常用的浏览器的新版本都使用了
     <code>
      window.requestAnimationFrame
     </code>
     方法。不过火狐老版本用的是
     <code>
      window.mozRequestAnimationFrame
     </code>
     ，Safari 老版本和 Chrome 用的是
     <code>
      window.webkitRequestAnimationFrame
     </code>
     。您希望尽可能少地处理特定于浏览器的代码，所以让我们想出一种方法，使用更快的方法来运行游戏循环，而不必了解不同浏览器制作和版本使用的不同方法。因为大多数浏览器已经使用了
     <code>
      window.requestAnimationFrame
     </code>
     方法，您可以如下扩展该方法的定义:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">window<span class="token punctuation">.</span>requestAnimationFrame <span class="token operator">=</span> window<span class="token punctuation">.</span>requestAnimationFrame <span class="token operator">||</span>
    window<span class="token punctuation">.</span>webkitRequestAnimationFrame <span class="token operator">||</span> window<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mozRequestAnimationFrame <span class="token operator">||</span>
    window<span class="token punctuation">.</span>oRequestAnimationFrame <span class="token operator">||</span> window<span class="token punctuation">.</span>msRequestAnimationFrame <span class="token operator">||</span>
    <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">callback</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        window<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setTimeout</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>callback<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1000</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您在这里使用
     <code>
      ||
     </code>
     操作符来确定
     <code>
      window.requestAnimationFrame
     </code>
     名称所指的方法。如果没有定义第一个选项(例如，如果您正在使用一个较旧的浏览器)，您将检查任何较旧的名称。如果没有优化的游戏循环方法可用，你让
     <code>
      requestAnimationFrame
     </code>
     指向一个调用
     <code>
      window.setTimeout
     </code>
     方法的函数。在 JavaScript 中，
     <code>
      window
     </code>
     变量是一个全局名称空间的容器。这意味着您可以调用前面有或没有
     <code>
      window
     </code>
     变量的
     <code>
      requestAnimationFrame
     </code>
     方法。电话:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">window<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">requestAnimationFrame</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>callbackFunction<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     相当于
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token function">requestAnimationFrame</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>callbackFunction<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     Painter3 示例使用优化的游戏循环方法来运行素材加载循环和游戏循环，如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">assetLoadingLoop</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>spritesStillLoading <span class="token operator">&gt;</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        window<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">requestAnimationFrame</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>assetLoadingLoop<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">initialize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">mainLoop</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     同样，下面是
     <code>
      Game
     </code>
     对象中的
     <code>
      mainLoop
     </code>
     方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">mainLoop</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">update</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reset</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    window<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">requestAnimationFrame</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mainLoop<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     浏览器以不同的方式处理事情是 JavaScript 开发人员面临的一个主要挑战，尽管在浏览器如何执行 JavaScript 代码的标准化方面已经取得了很大进展。当您开发 JavaScript 游戏时，您可能会在某个时候在浏览器中遇到这些差异。因此，在发布游戏之前，一定要在最常用的浏览器上测试你的游戏！
    </p>
    <p>
     将通用代码与游戏专用代码分开
    </p>
    <p>
     以前，你没有区分可以用于许多不同游戏的代码和特定于一个游戏的代码。您编写的一些代码，比如
     <code>
      Game.mainLoop
     </code>
     方法，可能对其他 JavaScript 游戏也有用。这同样适用于您编写的所有加载精灵的代码。既然您已经看到了在不同脚本文件上分割代码的方法，那么您可以利用这一点。通过将通用代码从特定于 Painter 的代码中分离出来，以后重用该通用代码将会更加容易。如果你想重用加载精灵的代码，你只需将包含代码的源文件包含到你的新游戏应用中，而不是在画师游戏代码中寻找你需要的。这样做的另一个原因是为了让你以后能更快地创建类似的游戏。你可能会发现自己正在开发一个与你之前开发的游戏相似的游戏。通过以这种方式组织代码，您可以更快地开发出新游戏，同时也不会重新发明轮子。
    </p>
    <p>
     Painter4 示例创建了一个单独的
     <code>
      Game.js
     </code>
     文件，其中包含了
     <code>
      Game
     </code>
     对象和许多属于该对象的有用方法。专用于 Painter 的零件已被移到
     <code>
      Painter.js
     </code>
     文件中。在这个文件中，有一个加载精灵的方法和一个初始化游戏的方法。此外，一个名为
     <code>
      PainterGameWorld.js
     </code>
     的新文件处理游戏中的各种对象。在以前版本的 Painter 中，这个游戏世界只包含一个背景图像和一门大炮。在下一节中，您将向这个游戏世界添加一个
     <em>
      球
     </em>
     。然后，画家游戏世界由一个对象定义，该对象确保所有游戏对象都被更新和绘制。这是
     <code>
      painterGameWorld
     </code>
     对象定义的一部分:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> painterGameWorld <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

painterGameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">handleInput</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">delta</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

painterGameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">update</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">delta</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">update</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">update</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

painterGameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">draw</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">drawImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     当你初始化游戏时，你初始化游戏对象，你告诉
     <code>
      Game
     </code>
     对象管理游戏世界的对象是
     <code>
      painterGameWorld
     </code>
     ，如下:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">initialize</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">initialize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">initialize</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld <span class="token operator">=</span> painterGameWorld<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在
     <code>
      Game.mainLoop
     </code>
     方法中，你现在只需要确保在
     <code>
      gameWorld
     </code>
     变量(它指的是
     <code>
      painterGameWorld
     </code>
     )上调用正确的方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">mainLoop</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">update</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">clear</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reset</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token function">requestAnimationFrame</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mainLoop<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     因此，你已经很好地分离了一般的游戏代码(在
     <code>
      Game.js
     </code>
     中)和特定于游戏的代码，包括加载精灵和初始化游戏(
     <code>
      Painter.js
     </code>
     )以及更新和绘制画师游戏对象(
     <code>
      PainterGameWorld.js
     </code>
     )。任何其他特定于 Painter 的游戏对象都是在各自的脚本文件中定义的(比如
     <code>
      Cannon.js
     </code>
     )。
    </p>
    <p>
     给游戏世界添加一个球
    </p>
    <p>
     在前面的章节中，您看到了如何通过加载单独的 JavaScript 文件、将通用游戏代码与特定于画师的代码分开、正确加载资源以及创建更高效的游戏循环来使您的 JavaScript 游戏应用更加灵活和高效。在本节中，您将通过添加一个由
     <code>
      cannon
     </code>
     对象射出的球来扩展画师游戏。为此，您添加一个
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象。
    </p>
    <p>
     您以与
     <code>
      cannon
     </code>
     对象非常相似的方式设置了
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象。在 Painter4 的例子中，你看到了一个 Painter 游戏的版本，它给游戏世界增加了一个球(见图 7-1 )。通过点击游戏屏幕上的任何地方，球都可以从大炮中射出。而且，球会随着大炮一起变色。您可以在
     <code>
      Ball.js
     </code>
     文件中找到描述
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象的代码。就像
     <code>
      cannon
     </code>
     对象一样，
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     由许多变量组成，比如位置、球的当前颜色和球精灵的来源。因为球在移动，你还需要存储它的
     <em>
      速度
     </em>
     。这个速度是一个矢量，定义了球的位置如何随时间变化。例如，如果球的速度为(0，1)，那么每秒钟，球的 y 位置增加 1 个像素(意味着球落下)。最后，球可以有两种状态:要么是因为从大炮中射出而在空中飞行，要么是等待被射出(所以它不动)。为此，您向
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象添加一个额外的布尔变量
     <code>
      shooting
     </code>
     。这是
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象结构的完整定义:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> ball <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">initialize</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">65</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">390</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>origin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     <img alt="9781430265382_Fig07-01.jpg" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/9ee7d7454b894a1fdacad644514ebb08.jpeg"/>
    </p>
    <p>
     图 7-1 。
     <em>
      包含炮管和飞行球
     </em>
     的画师 4
     <em>
      例子的截图
     </em>
    </p>
    <p>
     在你在本书中开发的游戏中，大多数物体都有位置和速度。因为这本书只涉及 2D 游戏，所以位置和速度都是由一个
     <code>
      x
     </code>
     和一个
     <code>
      y
     </code>
     变量组成的变量。当你更新这些游戏对象时，你需要根据速度向量和经过的时间来计算新的位置。在本章的后面，你会看到如何做到这一点。
    </p>
    <p>
     为了能够使用
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象，你需要更多的精灵。在
     <code>
      Game.``loadAssets
     </code>
     方法中，你加载红色、绿色和蓝色的球精灵。根据加农炮的颜色，你可以在以后改变球的颜色。这是扩展的
     <code>
      loadAssets
     </code>
     方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">loadAssets</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">var</span> <span class="token function-variable function">loadSprite</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">sprite</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"../../assets/Painter/sprites/"</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> sprite<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_background.jpg"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_barrel <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_cannon_barrel.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_cannon_red.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_cannon_green.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_blue <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_cannon_blue.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_ball_red.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_green <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_ball_green.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_blue <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">loadSprite</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"spr_ball_blue.png"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这里，您可以看到在 JavaScript 中使 sprite 加载调用更具可读性的一种好方法。您声明了一个引用函数的局部变量
     <code>
      loadSprite
     </code>
     。该函数将 sprite 图像名称作为参数，并调用
     <code>
      Game.loadSprite
     </code>
     方法。作为该方法的一个参数，您可以传递 sprite 的文件夹路径和 sprite 的名称。最后，该函数返回
     <code>
      Game.loadSprite
     </code>
     方法的结果。
    </p>
    <p>
     创造球
    </p>
    <p>
     让我们回到
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象。在那个对象的
     <code>
      initialize
     </code>
     方法中，你必须给成员变量赋值，就像在
     <code>
      cannon
     </code>
     对象中一样。当游戏开始时，球不应该移动。因此，你把球的速度设为零。此外，您最初将球设置到零位置。这样，它就藏在大炮后面，所以当球不动的时候，你看不见它。您最初将球的颜色设置为红色，并将
     <code>
      shooting
     </code>
     成员变量设置为
     <code>
      false
     </code>
     。下面是完整的方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">initialize</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>origin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在
     <code>
      initialize
     </code>
     方法旁边，您还添加了一个
     <code>
      reset
     </code>
     方法，用于重置球的位置及其射门状态:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">reset</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     当球从大炮中射出后飞出屏幕时，您可以通过调用此方法来重置它。此外，您向
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象添加了一个
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     方法。如果球没有投篮，你不想让球员看到它。因此，只有当球正在射击时，才绘制球精灵:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">draw</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">drawImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">,</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">,</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rotation<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>origin<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     你可以在这个方法的主体中看到，只有在球不投篮的时候，你才使用
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     关键字来画球。在
     <code>
      painterGameWorld
     </code>
     对象中，你必须调用球上的游戏循环方法。例如，这是
     <code>
      painterGameWorld
     </code>
     中的
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     方法，由此调用
     <code>
      ball.draw
     </code>
     方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">painterGameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">draw</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">drawImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     请注意游戏对象的绘制顺序:首先是背景图像，然后是球，然后是大炮。
    </p>
    <p>
     投篮
    </p>
    <p>
     玩家可以在游戏画面中点击鼠标左键射出一个彩球。球的速度和移动方向由玩家点击的位置决定。球应该向那个位置的方向移动；玩家离大炮越远，球的速度就越高。这是用户控制球的速度的直观方式。无论何时你设计一个游戏，都要仔细考虑用户的指令是如何被接收的，以及最自然或有效的处理方式是什么。
    </p>
    <p>
     为了处理输入，您向
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     对象添加了一个
     <code>
      handleInput
     </code>
     方法。在这个方法中，你可以通过使用
     <code>
      Mouse
     </code>
     对象来检查玩家是否点击了左键:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span>leftPressed<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">// do something...</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     然而，因为在任何时候都只能有一个球在空中，所以只有当球还没有在空中时，你才想做些什么。这意味着你必须检查球的投篮状态。如果球已经射出了，你就不必处理鼠标点击。所以，你用一个额外的条件来扩展你的
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令，这个额外的条件是球当前不在空中:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span>leftPressed <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="token operator">!</span>ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token comment">// do something...</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     如您所见，您将两个逻辑操作符(
     <code>
      &amp;&amp;
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      !
     </code>
     )结合使用。由于逻辑
     <em>
      而非
     </em>
     (
     <code>
      !
     </code>
     )运算符，只有当
     <code>
      shooting
     </code>
     变量的值为
     <code>
      false
     </code>
     时，
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令中的整个条件才会计算为
     <code>
      true
     </code>
     :换句话说，球当前没有射门。
    </p>
    <p>
     在
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令中，您需要做几件事情。你知道玩家点击了某个地方，球必须从大炮中射出。您需要做的第一件事是将变量
     <code>
      shooting
     </code>
     设置为正确的值，因为球的状态需要更改为“当前正在射门”:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     因为球现在正在移动，你需要给它一个
     <em>
      速度
     </em>
     。这个速度是玩家点击位置方向的向量。你可以通过鼠标位置减去球的位置来计算这个方向。因为速度有一个 x 分量和一个 y 分量，所以需要对两个维度都这样做:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">-</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">-</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     以这种方式计算速度也给出了期望的效果，即当用户点击离大炮更远时，速度更大，因为这样鼠标位置和球位置之间的差异也更大。然而，如果你现在玩这个游戏，球会移动得有点慢。因此，你将这个速度乘以一个常数值，这个常数值给出了球在这个游戏中可用的速度:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">-</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">1.2</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Mouse<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">-</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">1.2</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     我在测试了不同数值的游戏玩法后，选择了常量值 1.2。每款游戏都有许多这样的
     <em>
      游戏参数
     </em>
     ，你需要在游戏测试时调整这些参数以确定它们的最佳值。为这些参数找到正确的值对于一个玩得好的平衡游戏来说是至关重要的，你需要确保你选择的值不会使游戏过于容易或困难。例如，如果选择 0.3 而不是 1.2 这个常量值，球的移动速度会慢得多。这将使比赛变得更加困难，甚至可能使比赛无法进行，因为球可能永远也不能到达最远的地方。
    </p>
    <p>
     如果您将
     <code>
      handleInput
     </code>
     方法添加到
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     中，它不会被自动调用。您需要在
     <code>
      painterGameWorld
     </code>
     对象中显式地这样做。因此，您向该对象的
     <code>
      handleInput
     </code>
     方法添加了一条额外的指令:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">painterGameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">handleInput</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     更新球
    </p>
    <p>
     在对象中将相关的变量和方法组合在一起的一个很大的优点是，您可以保持每个对象相对较小和清晰。您可以设计或多或少反映游戏中各种游戏对象的对象。在这种情况下，你有一个大炮和球的对象。目标是每个游戏对象处理与该对象相关的玩家输入。你也想让游戏对象自己更新和绘制。这就是你给
     <code>
      ball
     </code>
     增加了一个
     <code>
      update
     </code>
     方法和一个
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     方法的原因，所以你可以在
     <code>
      painterGameWorld
     </code>
     的游戏循环方法中调用这些方法。
    </p>
    <p>
     在
     <code>
      ball.update
     </code>
     里面，你需要定义球的行为。根据球当前是否正在射门，这种行为是不同的。这是完整的方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">update</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">delta</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">0.99</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">+</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">*</span> delta<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">*</span> delta<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
            ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">else</span>
            ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">ballPosition</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">-</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>width <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">-</span> ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>height <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>painterGameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">isOutsideWorld</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reset</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     正如您在这个方法的头文件中看到的，它有一个名为
     <code>
      delta
     </code>
     的参数。这个参数是必要的，因为为了计算球的新位置，你需要知道从上一次调用
     <code>
      update
     </code>
     到现在已经过了多长时间。这个参数在一些游戏对象的
     <code>
      handleInput
     </code>
     方法中也很有用——例如，如果你想知道玩家移动鼠标的速度，那么你需要知道已经过了多长时间。Painter4 示例扩展了每个具有游戏循环方法(
     <code>
      handleInput
     </code>
     、
     <code>
      update
     </code>
     、
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     )的对象，以便将自上次更新以来经过的时间作为参数传递。
    </p>
    <p>
     但是 delta 的值在哪里计算呢？你是怎么计算的？在本例中，您在
     <code>
      Game.mainLoop
     </code>
     方法中这样做:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">mainLoop</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">var</span> delta <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">1</span> <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">60</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleInput</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">update</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">clear</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
