     为了在屏幕上绘制油漆桶，您向
     <code>
      PaintCan
     </code>
     类添加一个
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     方法，该方法简单地在期望的位置绘制油漆桶精灵。在
     <code>
      PainterGameWorld
     </code>
     类中，您调用不同游戏对象上的
     <code>
      handleInput
     </code>
     、
     <code>
      update
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     方法。例如
     <code>
      PainterGameWorld
     </code>
     中的
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     方法如下:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">PainterGameWorld</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">draw</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">drawImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>can1<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>can2<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>can3<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">draw</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     Painter5 示例的所有代码都可以在本章的示例文件夹中找到。图 8-1 显示了油漆工人 5 示例的屏幕截图，现在有三个掉落的油漆罐。
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="9781430265382_Fig08-01.jpg" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/8edb07efdbed21746a0c5d246cf78129.jpeg"/>
    </p>
    <p>
     图 8-1 。画家 5 示例的屏幕截图，其中有一门大炮、一个球和三个掉落的颜料罐
    </p>
    <p>
     将位置和速度表示为矢量
    </p>
    <p>
     您已经看到，类是一个有价值的概念，因为它们定义了对象的结构，以及通过方法修改这些对象的行为。当您需要多个相似的对象(例如三个油漆桶)时，这尤其有用。类非常有用的另一个领域是定义基本的数据结构和操作这些结构的方法。你已经见过的一个常见结构是一个表示二维位置或速度向量的对象:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> anotherPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">35</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">40</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     不幸的是，下面的指令是不允许的:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> sum <span class="token operator">=</span> position <span class="token operator">+</span> anotherPosition<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     原因是加法运算符不是为这样的复合对象定义的。当然，您可以定义一个方法来完成这项工作。但是其他一些方法也是有用的。例如，如果你能减去这些向量，乘以它们，计算它们的长度，等等，那就太好了。为了做到这一点，让我们创建一个
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     类。首先定义构造函数:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> x<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> y<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您现在可以创建一个对象，如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     如果你能初始化一个向量而不需要一直传递两个参数，那就太好了。一种方法是检查
     <code>
      x
     </code>
     和/或
     <code>
      y
     </code>
     是否未定义。如果是这种情况，只需将成员变量初始化为 0，如下:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">typeof</span> x <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> x<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">typeof</span> y <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> y<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在 JavaScript 中使用
     <code>
      typeof
     </code>
     关键字来返回变量的类型。这里你用它来检查
     <code>
      x
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      y
     </code>
     是否有一个已定义的类型。如果是这种情况，可以将作为参数传递的值赋给成员变量。否则，将值指定为 0。JavaScript 知道写下这种
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令的一个更简短的版本。这是相同方法的样子，只是缩短了:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> x <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> x <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> y <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> y <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     这段代码做的事情与带有完整的
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令的版本完全一样，但是它要短得多。问号前面是条件。然后，在问号后面，有两个值的选项，用冒号隔开。当使用这个较短的版本时，请确保您的代码仍然可读。本书仅使用较短的版本来检查参数是否已定义。这有好处；例如，您可以用各种方式创建
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     对象:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (0, 0)</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> anotherPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">35</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">40</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (35, 40)</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> yetAnotherPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">-</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (-1, 0)</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     现在你可以给
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     类添加一些有用的方法，这样用向量进行计算就变得更容易了。例如，下面的方法制作一个 vector 的副本:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">copy</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     如果你想从不同的游戏对象中复制位置或速度，这很方便。此外，比较矢量也很有用。
     <code>
      equals
     </code>
     方法为你做了这个:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">equals</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">obj</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">===</span> obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">===</span> obj<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您还可以定义一些基本操作，如向量的加、减、乘和除。首先，让我们定义一个向现有向量添加向量的方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">addTo</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">v</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您可以按如下方式使用此方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (10, 10)</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> anotherPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (20, 20)</span>
position<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTo</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>anotherPosition<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// now represents the vector (30, 30)</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     <code>
      addTo
     </code>
     方法的最后一条指令返回
     <code>
      this
     </code>
     。原因是你可以做所谓的
     <em>
      操作符链接
     </em>
     。因为
     <code>
      addTo
     </code>
     方法返回一个向量作为结果，所以您可以对该结果调用方法。例如:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (10, 10)</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> anotherPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (20, 20)</span>
position<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTo</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>anotherPosition<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTo</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>anotherPosition<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// position now represents the vector (50, 50)</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     根据传递给
     <code>
      addTo
     </code>
     方法的参数的类型，您可以做一些不同的事情。如果参数是一个数字，你只需把这个数字加到向量的每个元素上。如果它是一个向量，你用已经描述过的方法执行运算。一种方法是使用您之前见过的
     <code>
      typeof
     </code>
     操作符，如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">addTo</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">v</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">typeof</span> v <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token string">'Vector2'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">typeof</span> v <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token string">'Number'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您使用一个
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令来确定被传递的参数的类型，并相应地执行加法操作。另一种确定类型的方法是使用
     <code>
      constructor
     </code>
     变量，它是 JavaScript 中每个对象的一部分(就像
     <code>
      prototype
     </code>
     是每个函数的一部分一样)。这是
     <code>
      addTo
     </code>
     方法的一个版本，它使用了
     <code>
      constructor
     </code>
     变量，而不是
     <code>
      typeof
     </code>
     运算符:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">addTo</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">v</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>constructor <span class="token operator">===</span> Vector2<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>v<span class="token punctuation">.</span>constructor <span class="token operator">===</span> Number<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> v<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     <code>
      addTo
     </code>
     方法将一个向量添加到一个现有的向量中。您还可以定义一个
     <code>
      add
     </code>
     方法，将两个向量相加并返回一个
     <em>
      新向量
     </em>
     。为此，您可以重用
     <code>
      copy
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      addTo
     </code>
     方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">add</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">v</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">var</span> result <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">copy</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> result<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTo</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>v<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您现在可以执行以下操作:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (10, 10)</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> anotherPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">20</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// create a vector (20, 20)</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> sum <span class="token operator">=</span> position<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>anotherPosition<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// creates a new vector (30, 30)</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在本例中，
     <code>
      position
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      anotherPosition
     </code>
     在第三条指令中保持不变。创建一个新的 vector 对象，它包含操作数向量中值的总和。
    </p>
    <p>
     看看 Painter6 示例中的
     <code>
      Vector2.js
     </code>
     文件，在这里可以看到
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     类的完整定义。它定义了这个类中最常见的向量运算，包括本节讨论的加法方法。因此，在画师游戏中使用矢量要容易得多。
    </p>
    <p>
     在所有游戏对象中使用
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     类型来表示位置和速度。例如，这是
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     类的新构造函数:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Ball</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>origin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>shooting <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     感谢
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     类中的方法，您可以根据球的速度直观地更新球的位置，只需一行代码:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTo</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>velocity<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">multiply</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>delta<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     参数的默认值
    </p>
    <p>
     在完成本章之前，让我们再看一下
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     构造函数是如何定义的:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">x<span class="token punctuation">,</span> y</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> x <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> x <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> y <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> y <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     由于方法体内部的赋值指令，即使您在调用构造函数方法时没有传递任何参数，您仍将创建一个有效的
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     对象。如果没有定义参数
     <code>
      x
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      y
     </code>
     ，则使用
     <em>
      默认值
     </em>
     。您可以利用这种情况，因为依赖默认值可以简化代码编写。举个例子，这是在屏幕上绘制背景图像的指令:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">drawImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">x</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">y</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     通过让
     <code>
      drawImage
     </code>
     方法 自动为位置、旋转和原点参数提供默认值，可以使这个方法调用更加简洁:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Canvas2D_Singleton</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">drawImage</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">sprite<span class="token punctuation">,</span> position<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                                                   rotation<span class="token punctuation">,</span> origin</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> position <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> position <span class="token operator">:</span> Vector2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>zero<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    rotation <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> rotation <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> rotation <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    origin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">typeof</span> origin <span class="token operator">!==</span> <span class="token string">'undefined'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> origin <span class="token operator">:</span> Vector2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>zero<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token comment">// remaining drawing code here</span>
    <span class="token operator">...</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     然后绘制背景，如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Canvas2D<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">drawImage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>background<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     虽然参数的默认值在创建紧凑的代码时非常有用，但是请确保您总是为您的方法提供文档，指定如果方法的调用方没有提供所有参数时将使用哪些默认值。
    </p>
    <p>
     你学到了什么
    </p>
    <p>
     在本章中，您学习了:
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      如何使用原型机制定义类
     </li>
     <li>
      如何创建一个类型/类的多个实例
     </li>
     <li>
      如何增加游戏的随机性以增加可玩性
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h2>
     <a id="_1437">
     </a>
     九、颜色和碰撞
    </h2>
    <p>
     到目前为止，您已经实现了 Painter 游戏的很大一部分。您已经看到了如何使用原型机制定义游戏对象类。通过使用这些类，您可以更好地控制游戏对象的结构以及如何创建特定类型的游戏对象。您将这些类定义分隔在不同的文件中。这样，当你在未来的游戏中需要一个具有相同行为的大炮或球时，你可以简单地复制这些文件并在你的游戏中创建这些游戏对象的实例。
    </p>
    <p>
     当您更仔细地查看类的定义时，您会发现类定义了对象的内部结构(它由哪些变量组成)以及以某种方式操作该对象的方法。这些方法可以帮助更精确地定义一个对象的可能性和局限性。例如，如果有人想重用
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     类，他们不需要很多关于球是如何构造的详细信息。简单地创建一个实例并调用 game-loop 方法就足以在游戏中添加一个飞行球。一般来说，当你设计一个程序时，无论是游戏还是完全不同的应用，清楚地定义某个类的对象的可能性是很重要的。方法是做到这一点的一种方式。本章向你展示了另一种定义对象可能性的方法:通过定义
     <em>
      属性
     </em>
     。本章还介绍了一种表示颜色的类型，并展示了如何处理球和颜料罐之间的碰撞(如果发生这种情况，颜料罐需要改变颜色)。
    </p>
    <p>
     表现颜色的不同方式
    </p>
    <p>
     在 Painter 的早期版本中，您已经相当实际地处理了颜色。例如，在
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     类中，您通过使用
     <code>
      currentColor
     </code>
     变量跟踪当前颜色，该变量最初指向红色的 cannon sprite:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     你在
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     类中做了类似的事情，除了你让同名的变量指向彩色的球精灵。虽然这样做很好，但当球的颜色需要根据大炮的颜色而改变时，这就有点不方便了:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">else</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这个
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令中，你需要处理所有三种不同的颜色；此外，现在
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     类需要了解
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     类使用的精灵。如果可以更统一地定义颜色，并在所有游戏对象类中使用该定义来表示不同的颜色，不是更好吗？当然会！现在开始在游戏中统一颜色使用的另一个原因是，如果你决定增加游戏中可能的颜色数量(到 4、6、10 或更多)，当前的方法将需要更长的编程时间。
    </p>
    <p>
     属于本章的 Painter7 示例添加了一个
     <code>
      Color.js
     </code>
     JavaScript 文件。要定义不同的颜色，可以使用与定义不同键类似的方法。这个文件定义了一个名为
     <code>
      Color
     </code>
     的变量。
     <code>
      Color
     </code>
     变量包含许多子变量，每个子变量代表一种不同的颜色。您可以如下定义颜色:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> Color <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">red</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">blue</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">yellow</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">green</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token comment">// and so on</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     然而，这种方法并不是一个好的解决方案。用数字来表示颜色并不是一个坏主意，但是你不应该自己编一个没有人知道的编号方案。在 HTML 中已经有了一个定义颜色的标准，它使用以十六进制形式表示的整数，您也可以使用这个标准。好处是这种方法被广泛使用，被广泛理解，被工具广泛支持(比如 Adobe 的 Kuler，比如 at
     <code>
      http://kuler.adobe.com
     </code>
     )。
    </p>
    <p>
     在 HTML 标准中，您可以通过使用十六进制表示来定义网页中元素的颜色。例如:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token operator">&lt;</span>body style<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token string">"background: #0000FF"</span><span class="token operator">&gt;</span>
That's a very nice background<span class="token punctuation">.</span>
<span class="token operator">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">/</span>body<span class="token operator">&gt;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     在这种情况下，您指定主体的背景颜色应该是颜色
     <em>
      蓝色
     </em>
     。十六进制表示让您定义红、绿、蓝(RGB)值中的颜色，其中
     <em>
      00
     </em>
     表示没有颜色分量，
     <em>
      FF
     </em>
     表示颜色分量最大。
    </p>
    <p>
     <code>
      #
     </code>
     符号不是数字的一部分，它只是向浏览器表明后面是十六进制数而不是十进制数。所以，
     <code>
      #0000FF
     </code>
     十六进制数代表蓝色，
     <code>
      #00FF00
     </code>
     是绿色，
     <code>
      #FF0000
     </code>
     是红色。当然，颜色分量的任何混合或渐变都可以用类似的方式来定义。
     <code>
      #808080
     </code>
     为灰色，
     <code>
      #800080
     </code>
     为紫色，
     <code>
      #FF00FF
     </code>
     为洋红色。
    </p>
    <p>
     下面是
     <code>
      Color
     </code>
     变量的一部分:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> Color <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">aliceBlue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#F0F8FF"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">antiqueWhite</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#FAEBD7"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">aqua</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#00FFFF"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">aquamarine</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#7FFFD4"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">azure</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#F0FFFF"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">beige</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#F5F5DC"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">bisque</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#FFE4C4"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">black</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#000000"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">blanchedAlmond</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#FFEBCD"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">blue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#0000FF"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">blueViolet</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#8A2BE2"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">brown</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">"#A52A2A"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token comment">// and so on</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     有关更完整的颜色列表，请参见
     <code>
      Color.js
     </code>
     文件。您现在可以开始在您的类中使用这些颜色定义。
    </p>
    <p>
     对象的受控数据访问
    </p>
    <p>
     三个游戏对象类代表一个特定颜色的对象:
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     、
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      PaintCan
     </code>
     。为了简单起见，让我们从如何修改
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     类来使用上一节中的颜色定义开始。到目前为止，
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     构造函数看起来是这样的:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">72</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">405</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>colorPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">55</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">388</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>origin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">34</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">34</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>rotation <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您可以做的是添加另一个成员变量，给出加农炮的当前颜色。因此，新的
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     构造函数如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">72</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">405</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>colorPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">55</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">388</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>origin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">34</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">34</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>color <span class="token operator">=</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>rotation <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     然而，这并不理想。您现在存储了冗余数据，因为颜色信息由两个变量表示。此外，当加农炮的颜色改变时，如果您忘记改变两个变量中的一个，您可能会以这种方式引入错误。
    </p>
    <p>
     另一种方法是不存储对当前 sprite 的引用。这将是构造函数:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">72</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">405</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>colorPosition <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">55</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">388</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>origin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">34</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">34</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>color <span class="token operator">=</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>rotation <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     这也不是一种理想的方法，因为每次调用
     <code>
      draw
     </code>
     方法时，您都需要查找正确的 sprite。
    </p>
    <p>
     一个解决方案是定义两个方法，允许
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     类的用户检索和设置颜色信息。然后，您可以保持构造函数不变，但添加方法来读取和写入颜色值。例如，您可以将以下两个方法添加到
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     原型中:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token class-name">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">getColor</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function-variable function">setColor</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     现在
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     类的用户不需要知道在内部，您使用一个 sprite 来确定大炮的当前颜色。用户可以简单地传递颜色定义来读取或写入加农炮的颜色:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">myCannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setColor</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">var</span> cannonColor <span class="token operator">=</span> myCannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getColor</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     有时，程序员称这类方法为
     <em>
      getter
     </em>
     和
     <em>
      setter
     </em>
     。在许多面向对象的编程语言中，方法是访问对象内部数据的唯一方式，因此对于每个需要在类外部访问的成员变量，程序员都添加了一个 getter 和一个 setter。JavaScript 提供了一个对面向对象编程语言来说相对较新的特性:
     <em>
      属性
     </em>
     。属性是 getter 和 setter 的替代品。它定义了从对象中检索数据时会发生什么，以及向对象内部的数据赋值时会发生什么。
    </p>
    <p>
     只读属性
    </p>
    <p>
     按照基于原型的编程范式，您希望能够向类添加属性。JavaScript 有一个叫做
     <code>
      defineProperty
     </code>
     的简便方法可以让你做到这一点。这个方法是对象的一部分，俗称
     <code>
      Object
     </code>
     。
     <code>
      Object
     </code>
     还有几个其他有用的方法，您稍后会了解到。
     <code>
      defineProperty
     </code>
     方法需要三个参数:
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      应添加属性的原型(例如，
      <code>
       Cannon.prototype
      </code>
      )
     </li>
     <li>
      属性的名称(例如，
      <code>
       color
      </code>
      )
     </li>
     <li>
      一个最多包含两个变量的对象:
      <code>
       get
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       set
      </code>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <code>
      get
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      set
     </code>
     变量都应该指向一个函数，该函数应该在属性被读取或写入时被执行。然而，可以只定义一个
     <code>
      get
     </code>
     或
     <code>
      set
     </code>
     零件。如果属性只读取信息而不能更改信息，这将非常有用。如果一个属性只读取信息，它被称为
     <em>
      只读属性
     </em>
     。下面是一个简单的例子，它是您添加到
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     类中的只读属性:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Object<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">defineProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"center"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">get</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>width <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>height <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     如您所见，您向
     <code>
      defineProperty
     </code>
     方法提供了三个参数:原型、名称和对象。这个楼盘的名字叫
     <code>
      center
     </code>
     。它的目标是提供代表大炮的精灵的中心。因为不可能改变中心的值，所以这个属性只有一个
     <code>
      get
     </code>
     部分。这反映在作为第三个参数传递的对象中，该对象包含一个指向函数的变量
     <code>
      get
     </code>
     。以下是使用该属性的方法:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> cannonCenter <span class="token operator">=</span> cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>center<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     很简单，不是吗？同样，您可以添加一个提供加农炮高度的属性，如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Object<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">defineProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"height"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">get</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>height<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     你甚至可以定义一个属性
     <code>
      ballPosition
     </code>
     来计算球应该在的位置:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Object<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">defineProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"ballPosition"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">get</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">var</span> opposite <span class="token operator">=</span> Math<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">sin</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>rotation<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">*</span>
                sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_barrel<span class="token punctuation">.</span>width <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">0.6</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">var</span> adjacent <span class="token operator">=</span> Math<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">cos</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>rotation<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">*</span>
                sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_barrel<span class="token punctuation">.</span>width <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token number">0.6</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">+</span> adjacent<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
                <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">+</span> opposite<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     就像处理方法一样，使用
     <code>
      this
     </code>
     关键字来引用属性所属的对象。属于本章的 Painter7 示例将属性添加到不同的类中。例如，
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     类也包含一个
     <code>
      center
     </code>
     属性。结合您添加到
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     中的便捷的方法，您现在可以在一行代码中根据大炮的旋转来计算球的新位置:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ballPosition<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">subtractFrom</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>center<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     定义类、方法和属性的好处是你的代码变得更短，更容易理解。例如，您还可以将以下属性添加到
     <code>
      Vector2
     </code>
     :
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Object<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">defineProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>Vector2<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"zero"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">get</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Vector2</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     现在你有一个非常简单的方法来创建一个二维向量，如下:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> position <span class="token operator">=</span> Vector2<span class="token punctuation">.</span>zero<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     从现在开始，我使用属性和方法来定义对象的行为和数据访问。通过在类中定义有用的属性和方法，游戏代码通常会变得更短，更容易阅读。例如，在您拥有包含有用方法和属性的类之前，您必须这样计算球的位置:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position <span class="token operator">=</span> Game<span class="token punctuation">.</span>gameWorld<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">ballPosition</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>x <span class="token operator">-</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>width <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>position<span class="token punctuation">.</span>y <span class="token operator">-</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor<span class="token punctuation">.</span>height <span class="token operator">/</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     正如您在本节前面所看到的，新的方法要短得多。这种效果在你在本书中开发的游戏代码中随处可见，我鼓励你接受类、方法和属性所提供的力量！
    </p>
    <p>
     检索加农炮的颜色
    </p>
    <p>
     在本章中，您定义了一个名为
     <code>
      Color
     </code>
     的新类型。因此，让我们结合使用该类型和属性来读取和写入大炮的颜色。根据
     <code>
      currentColor
     </code>
     变量指向的 sprite，您希望返回不同的颜色值。为了实现这一点，您需要在
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     类中添加一个名为
     <code>
      color
     </code>
     的属性。在该属性的
     <code>
      get
     </code>
     部分，您使用一个
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令来找出返回哪种颜色。就像有返回值的方法一样，使用
     <code>
      return
     </code>
     关键字来指示属性应该返回什么值:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Object<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">defineProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"color"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">get</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     现在，您可以使用该属性来访问加农炮的颜色。例如，您可以将它存储在一个变量中，如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js"><span class="token keyword">var</span> cannonColor <span class="token operator">=</span> cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Color<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     您还希望能够为加农炮颜色赋值。为此，您必须定义属性的
     <code>
      set
     </code>
     部分。在那个部分，您需要修改
     <code>
      currentColor
     </code>
     变量的值。当在另一个方法中使用该属性时，会提供此值。例如，它可能是这样的指令:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">cannon<span class="token punctuation">.</span>color <span class="token operator">=</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     同样，您使用一条
     <code>
      if
     </code>
     指令来确定
     <code>
      currentColor
     </code>
     变量的新值应该是什么。右边的赋值作为
     <em>
      参数
     </em>
     传递给
     <code>
      set
     </code>
     部件。完整的属性如下所示:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Object<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">defineProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Cannon</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"color"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">get</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">set</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>cannon_blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    <p>
     这是一个可以读写的属性示例。你添加一个
     <code>
      color
     </code>
     属性到所有的彩色游戏对象类型:
     <code>
      Cannon
     </code>
     、
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      PaintCan
     </code>
     。在
     <code>
      get
     </code>
     和
     <code>
      set
     </code>
     部分的代码中唯一的区别是用来表示颜色的精灵。例如，这是
     <code>
      Ball
     </code>
     类的
     <code>
      color
     </code>
     属性:
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-js">Object<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">defineProperty</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Ball</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>prototype<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"color"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">get</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">===</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span>
                <span class="token keyword">return</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
        <span class="token function-variable function">set</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>red<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_red<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>green<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
                <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentColor <span class="token operator">=</span> sprites<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ball_green<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>value <span class="token operator">===</span> Color<span class="token punctuation">.</span>blue<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
